Any line that doesn't start with TM/HM/SPECIES is discarded as a comment.
The TM move specified will automatically be written over the ARM9 entry as well.
The item icon and palette will still have to be modified, else the original type will be displayed.

Pokemon who don't naturally learn the move are separated at the bottom. Unless otherwise noted they are fully custom changes.

Inheritance for Gen 8/9 evolutions:
/*  Inherited TM006, TM010, TM023, TM045, TM077, TM083, TM087 from Stantler */
/*  Inherited TM006, TM010, TM020, TM045, TM047, TM087, HM001, HM006 from Scyther */
/*  Inherited TM001, TM006, TM010, TM041, TM045, TM052*, TM083, TM087 from Ursaring */
/* Inherited TM001, TM006, TM010, TM023, TM040, TM045, TM066, TM077, TM083, HM004, HM006, HM008 from Primeape */
/* Inherited TM006, TM010, TM023, TM045, TM049, TM077, TM083, TM087, HM004, HM006 from Girafarig */
/* Inherited TM006, TM010, TM023, TM045, TM057, TM073, TM077, TM087, TM090, HM004, HM006 from Dunsparce */
/* Inherited TM001, TM006, TM010, TM012, TM045, TM066, TM069, TM087, HM001, HM006 from Bisharp */
